{"id":"e92573fd-6811-4820-9777-8ab495a143e5","identifier":"FRG-222","title":"Interaction Slot System (Smart Objects)","description":"Objects must be service providers with capacity and reservation logic.

## Current Problem

Multiple characters can walk to and interact with the same object simultaneously. No conflict detection — tea_set can be 'used' by all 3 characters at once.

## Requirements

1. **Slots/Capacity:** Each object defines how many characters can use it simultaneously (e.g., bench=2, single chair=1, tea_set=1, kotatsu=2).
2. **Reservation:** Before walking to an object, character must request a reservation. Object returns available/busy.
3. **State Locking:** Once character arrives and begins interaction, slot is locked. Other characters checking that object get a 'busy' signal.
4. **Release:** When interaction ends (auto_next timer expires), slot is released.

## Acceptance Criteria

* Objects have configurable capacity (slots)
* Characters check availability before committing to an interaction
* If object is full, character receives busy signal and must choose differently
* Debug page shows slot occupancy per object

   206→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   207→
   208→class ObjectInstance {
   209→  constructor(def) {
   210→    this.id        = def.id;
   211→    this.name      = def.name;
   212→    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   213→    this.position  = def.position;
   214→    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   215→    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   216→    this.states    = def.states;
   217→    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   218→    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   219→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   220→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   221→  }
   222→
   223→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   224→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   225→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   226→  }
   227→
   228→  /**
   229→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   230→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   231→   */
   232→  interact(action = 'use') {
   233→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   234→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   235→    if (!tr) return null;
   236→
   237→    this.state = tr.next;
   238→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   239→
   240→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   241→    return {
   242→      objectId: this.id,
   243→      state:    this.state,
   244→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   245→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   246→    };
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  /**
   250→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   251→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   252→   */
   253→  tick(deltaMs) {
   254→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   255→
   256→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   257→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   258→
   259→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   260→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   261→
   262→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   263→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   264→
   265→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   266→    return {
   267→      objectId: this.id,
   268→      state:    this.state,
   269→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   270→      auto:     true,
   271→    };
   272→  }
   273→}
   274→
   275→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   276→
   277→export class ObjectEngine {
   278→  constructor() {
   279→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  addObjects(defs) {
   283→    for (const def of defs) {
   284→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   285→    }
   286→  }
   287→
   288→  /**
   289→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   290→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   291→   */
   292→  tick(deltaMs) {
   293→    const events = [];
   294→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   295→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   296→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   297→    }
   298→    return events;
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  /**
   302→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   303→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   304→   */
   305→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   306→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   307→  }
   308→
   309→  getAll()   { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   310→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   311→}

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   154→
   155→  get px() {
   156→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   157→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   158→    }
   159→    const next = this.path[0];
   160→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   161→  }
   162→
   163→  get py() {
   164→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   165→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   166→    }
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172→
   173→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   174→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   175→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   176→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   177→
   178→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   179→      this.path         = path;
   180→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   181→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   182→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   183→      this.action       = 'walking';
   184→
   185→      // Set initial facing from first step
   186→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   187→      this._playWalkAnim();
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   194→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   195→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   196→  }
   197→
   198→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   199→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   200→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   201→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   202→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   203→    if (this.sprite) {
   204→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   205→    }
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   209→
   210→  update(deltaMs) {
   211→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   212→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   213→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   214→
   215→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   216→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   217→
   218→      // Advance tiles
   219→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   220→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   221→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   222→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   224→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   225→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   226→      }
   227→
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action       = 'idle';
   231→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   232→        this._playAnim('idle');
   233→      } else {
   234→        this._playWalkAnim();
   235→      }
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   237→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   239→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   240→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   241→        this.action        = 'idle';
   242→        this.interactTarget = null;
   243→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   244→        this._playAnim('idle');
   245→      }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    // Tick dialogue
   249→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   250→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   251→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   252→    }
   253→
   254→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   255→    if (this.sprite) {
   256→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   257→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   261→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   262→    }
   263→  }
   264→
   265→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   268→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   269→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   270→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   271→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   272→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   273→    });
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   277→
   278→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   279→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   280→    const next = this.path[0];
   281→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   282→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   283→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   284→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   285→    } else {
   286→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   287→    }
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  _playAnim(type) {
   291→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   292→    const key = type === 'idle'
   293→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   294→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   295→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   296→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   297→    }
   298→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  _playWalkAnim() {
   302→    this._playAnim('walk');
   303→  }
   304→}

     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).

     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→

    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    67→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    68→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    69→      }
    70→
    71→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    72→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    73→        this._doWander(char);
    74→      }
    75→
    76→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    77→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    78→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    79→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    80→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    81→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    82→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    83→        }
    84→      }
    85→
    86→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    87→      char.update(deltaMs);
    88→    }
    89→  }
    90→
    91→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    92→
    93→  /**
    94→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    95→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    96→   */
    97→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    98→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    99→
   100→    if (event) {
   101→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   102→
   103→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   104→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   105→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   106→      if (obj && event.state) {
   107→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   108→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   109→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   110→        }
   111→      }
   112→
   113→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, holdMs);
   114→
   115→      if (event.speech) {
   116→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   117→      }
   118→
   119→      if (event.emoji) {
   120→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   121→      }
   122→    }
   123→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   124→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   125→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   126→  }
   127→
   128→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   129→
   130→  _doWander(char) {
   131→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   132→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   133→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   134→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   135→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   136→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   137→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   138→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   139→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   140→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   141→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   142→            return;
   143→          }
   144→        }
   145→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   146→      }
   147→    }
   148→
   149→    // Random walkable tile
   150→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   151→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   152→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   153→      return;
   154→    }
   155→
   156→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   157→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   158→
   159→    let moved = false;
   160→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   161→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   162→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   163→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   164→      if (moved) break;
   165→    }
   166→
   167→    if (!moved) {
   168→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   169→    }
   170→  }
   171→
   172→  /**
   173→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   174→   */
   175→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   176→    const dirs = [
   177→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   178→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   179→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   180→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   181→    ];
   182→    for (const d of dirs) {
   183→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   184→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   185→      }
   186→    }
   187→    return null;
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   191→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   192→    const tiles = [];
   193→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   194→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   195→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   196→      }
   197→    }

     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    54→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    77→
    78→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    79→        .filter(c => {
    80→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    81→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    82→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
    83→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    84→        })
    85→        .map(c => ({ label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
    86→
    87→      const systemPrompt =
    88→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    89→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    90→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    91→
    92→      const userPrompt =
    93→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    94→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    95→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    96→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    97→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
    98→        `Choose one action:
` +
    99→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   100→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   101→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   102→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_label", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }`;
   103→
   104→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   105→
   106→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   107→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   108→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   109→        model: this.model,
   110→        max_tokens: 256,
   111→        system: systemPrompt,
   112→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   113→      });
   114→
   115→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   116→
   117→      if (!res.ok) {
   118→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   119→        return;
   120→      }
   121→
   122→      const data = await res.json();
   123→
   124→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   125→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   126→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   127→              ?? null;
   128→
   129→      if (!text) {
   130→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   131→        return;
   132→      }
   133→
   134→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   135→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   136→    } catch (err) {
   137→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   138→    } finally {
   139→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   140→    }
   141→  }
   142→
   143→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   144→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   145→
   146→    switch (decision.action) {
   147→      case 'move':
   148→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   149→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   150→        }
   151→        break;
   152→
   153→      case 'interact': {
   154→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   155→        if (obj) {
   156→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   157→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   158→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   159→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   160→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   161→          }
   162→        }
   163→        break;
   164→      }
   165→
   166→      case 'idle':
   167→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   168→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   169→        break;
   170→
   171→      case 'talk': {
   172→        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);
   173→        if (target) {
   174→          // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B
   175→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   176→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   177→            // Initiator says something via speech bubble
   178→            if (decision.dialogue) {
   179→              character.pendingSpeech = decision.dialogue;
   180→            }
   181→            // Character B responds
   182→            if (decision.targetDialogue) {
   183→              target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;
   184→            }
   185→            // Queue conversation event for the debug log
   186→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   187→              simState.pushEvent({
   188→                type: 'conversation',
   189→                speakerLabel: character.label,
   190→                targetLabel: target.label,
   191→                dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
   192→                response: decision.targetDialogue || '',
   193→              });
   194→            }
   195→          }
   196→        }
   197→        break;
   198→      }
   199→    }
   200→
   201→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   202→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   203→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   204→    }
   205→
   206→    if (decision.description) {
   207→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   208→    }
   209→

   240→  <script type="module">
   241→    import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './src/objects.js';
   242→    import { SimulationEngine } from './src/Engine.js';
   243→    import { Character } from './src/Character.js';
   244→    import { AIEngine } from './src/AIEngine.js';
   245→
   246→    // ── Walkable grid (mirrors scene.js) ──────────────────────────────────────
   247→
   248→    const GRID_COLS = 19;
   249→    const GRID_ROWS = 13;
   250→
   251→    function buildWalkableGrid() {
   252→      const grid = [];
   253→      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
   254→        const r = [];
   255→        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
   256→          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
   257→        }
   258→        grid.push(r);
   259→      }
   260→      // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
   261→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   262→        const { tx, ty } = def.position;
   263→        if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
   264→          grid[ty][tx] = false;
   265→        }
   266→      }
   267→      return grid;
   268→    }
   269→
   270→    // ── Character definitions (mirrors scene.js) ─────────────────────────────
   271→
   272→    const CHARS_CONFIG = [
   273→      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,
   274→        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },
   275→      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,
   276→        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },
   277→      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 13, ty: 5,
   278→        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },
   279→    ];
   280→
   281→    // ── Engine setup ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   282→
   283→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   284→
   285→    const aiEngine = new AIEngine({
   286→      endpoint: '/api/llm',
   287→      model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   288→      decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,
   289→      onDecision: (char, decision, objects) => {
   290→        const targetName = decision.targetId
   291→          ? (objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId)?.name ?? decision.targetId)
   292→          : decision.targetTile
   293→            ? `(${decision.targetTile.tx},${decision.targetTile.ty})`
   294→            : decision.targetCharacter
   295→              ?? null;
   296→        pushAILog(char.label, decision.action, targetName, decision.dialogue);
   297→      },
   298→    });
   299→
   300→    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS, aiEngine });
   301→
   302→    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {
   303→      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({
   304→        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   305→      }));
   306→    }
   307→
   308→    // ── UI state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   309→
   310→    let paused = false;
   311→    let speed  = 1;
   312→    let lastTs = null;
   313→
   314→    // Event log (newest-first)
   315→    const log = [];
   316→    const MAX_LOG = 150;
   317→    let logDirty = false;
   318→
   319→    // Track previous object states so we can log from→to
   320→    const prevStateMap = new Map();
   321→    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   322→      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   323→    }
   324→
   325→    // ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   326→
   327→    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
   328→    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   329→      paused = !paused;
   330→      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';
   331→      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);
   332→      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume
   333→    });
   334→
   335→    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
   336→      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   337→        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);
   338→        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   339→        btn.classList.add('active');
   340→      });
   341→    });
   342→
   343→    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
   344→      // Reset object states to defaults
   345→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   346→        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);
   347→        if (!obj) continue;
   348→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';
   349→        obj._resetAutoTimer();
   350→        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);
   351→      }
   352→      // Reset sim clock
   353→      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   354→      // Clear log
   355→      log.length = 0;
   356→      logDirty = true;
   357→      // Update badge classes immediately
   358→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   359→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   360→      }
   361→    });
   362→
   363→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   364→
   365→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   366→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   367→    ]);
   368→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   369→
   370→    function badgeClass(state) {
   371→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   372→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   373→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   374→      return 'other';
   375→    }
   376→
   377→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   378→
   379→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   380→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   381→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   382→      logDirty = true;
   383→    }
   384→
   385→    function pushAILog(charLabel, action, target, dialogue) {
   386→      log.unshift({ type: 'ai', charLabel, action, target, dialogue, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   387→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   388→      logDirty = true;
   389→    }
   390→
   391→    // ── Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) ─────────────────────
   392→
   393→    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {
   394→      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   395→      if (!obj) return;
   396→      const from = obj.state;
   397→      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   398→      if (ev) {
   399→        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);
   400→        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);
   401→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   402→      }
   403→    };
   404→
   405→    // ── Build DOM cards (once) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   406→
   407→    function initObjectCards() {
   408→      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');
   409→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   410→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   411→        card.className = 'object-card';
   412→        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;
   413→        card.innerHTML = `
   414→          <div class="object-card-header">
   415→            <span class="object-name">${obj.name}</span>
   416→            <span class="state-badge" id="badge-${obj.id}"></span>
   417→          </div>
   418→          <div class="position-hint">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>
   419→          <div class="timer-bar" id="timerbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   420→            <div class="timer-fill" id="timerfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   421→          </div>
   422→          <div class="timer-text" id="timertext-${obj.id}" style="display:none"></div>
   423→          <div class="interactions" id="int-${obj.id}"></div>
   424→        `;
   425→        grid.appendChild(card);
   426→        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint
   427→      }
   428→    }
   429→
   430→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   431→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   432→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   433→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   434→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   435→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   436→      if (!badge) return;
   437→
   438→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   439→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   440→
   441→      if (stateChanged) {
   442→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   443→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   444→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   445→
   446→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   447→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   448→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   449→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   450→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   451→        ).join('');
   452→      }
   453→
   454→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   455→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   456→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   457→      if (hasTimer) {
   458→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   459→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   460→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   461→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   462→        timerText.style.display = '';
   463→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   464→      } else {
   465→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   466→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   467→      }
   468→    }
   469→
   470→    function initCharacterCards() {
   471→      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');
   472→      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
   473→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   474→        card.className = 'character-card';
   475→        card.id = `char-${i}`;
   476→        grid.appendChild(card);
   477→        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint
   478→      });
   479→    }
   480→
   481→    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {
   482→      const card = document.getElementById(`char-${i}`);
   483→      if (!card) return;
   484→
   485→      const targetName = char.interactTarget
   486→        ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)
   487→        : char.targetObjectId
   488→          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)
   489→          : '—';
   490→
   491→      // Hold countdown timer (shown while character is locked at an object)
   492→      let holdHtml = '';
   493→      if (char.action === 'interacting' && char.interactTimer > 0 && char.interactTimerMax > 0) {
   494→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - char.interactTimer / char.interactTimerMax) * 100));
   495→        holdHtml = `
   496→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   497→            <span>Hold</span>
   498→            <span class="char-value">${Math.ceil(char.interactTimer / 1000)}s</span>
   499→          </div>
   500→          <div class="stat-bar">
   501→            <div class="stat-fill hold-timer" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   502→          </div>
   503→        `;
   504→      }
   505→
   506→      // AI decision cooldown timer
   507→      let cooldownHtml = '';
   508→      if (aiEngine.enabled) {
   509→        const remaining  = Math.max(0, aiEngine._timers.get(char.name) ?? aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs);
   510→        const pct        = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - remaining / aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs) * 100));
   511→        const secRemaining = Math.ceil(remaining / 1000);
   512→        cooldownHtml = `
   513→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   514→            <span>AI next</span>
   515→            <span class="char-value">${secRemaining}s</span>
   516→          </div>
   517→          <div class="stat-bar">
   518→            <div class="stat-fill ai-cooldown" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   519→          </div>
   520→        `;
   521→      }
   522→
   523→      card.innerHTML = `
   524→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>
   525→        <div class="char-row">
   526→          <span>Action</span>
   527→          <span class="action-badge ${char.action}">${char.action}</span>
   528→        </div>
   529→        <div class="char-row">
   530→          <span>Position</span>
   531→          <span class="char-value">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>
   532→        </div>
   533→        <div class="char-row">
   534→          <span>Facing</span>
   535→          <span class="char-value">${char.facing}</span>
   536→        </div>
   537→        <div class="char-row">
   538→          <span>Target</span>
   539→          <span class="char-value">${targetName}</span>
   540→        </div>
   541→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   542→          <span>Mood</span>
   543→          <span class="char-value">${char.mood}</span>
   544→        </div>
   545→        <div class="stat-bar">
   546→          <div class="stat-fill mood" style="width:${char.mood}%"></div>
   547→        </div>
   548→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   549→          <span>Energy</span>
   550→          <span class="char-value">${char.energy}</span>
   551→        </div>
   552→        <div class="stat-bar">
   553→          <div class="stat-fill energy" style="width:${char.energy}%"></div>
   554→        </div>
   555→        ${holdHtml}
   556→        ${cooldownHtml}
   557→      `;
   558→    }
   559→
   560→    function renderEventLog() {
   561→      if (!logDirty) return;
   562→      logDirty = false;
   563→
   564→      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');
   565→      if (log.length === 0) {
   566→        el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div>';
   567→        return;
   568→      }
   569→      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => {
   570→        if (e.type === 'ai') {
   571→          const targetStr   = e.target   ? ` \u2192 ${e.target}` : '';
   572→          const dialogueStr = e.dialogue ? ` \u201c${e.dialogue}\u201d` : '';
   573→          return `
   574→            <div class="log-entry ai">
   575→              <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   576→              <span class="log-obj">${e.charLabel}</span>
   577→              <span class="log-transition">${e.action}${targetStr}${dialogueStr}</span>
   578→              <span class="log-tag ai">AI</span>
   579→            </div>
   580→          `;
   581→        }
   582→        return `
   583→          <div class="log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}">
   584→            <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   585→            <span class="log-obj">${e.objectId}</span>
   586→            <span class="log-transition">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>
   587→            <span class="log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}">${e.trigger}</span>
   588→          </div>
   589→        `;
   590→      }).join('');
   591→    }
   592→
   593→    // ── Tick loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   594→
   595→    function tick(ts) {
   596→      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   597→
   598→      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {
   599→        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;
   600→
   601→        // Snapshot states before update
   602→        const snap = new Map();
   603→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   604→
   605→        // Advance simulation
   606→        simEngine.update(realDelta);
   607→
   608→        // Detect auto-transitions
   609→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   610→          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {
   611→            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');
   612→            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   613→          }
   614→          updateObjectCard(obj);
   615→        }
   616→
   617→        // Update character cards
   618→        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));
   619→      }
   620→
   621→      lastTs = ts;
   622→
   623→      // Clock
   624→      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();
   625→
   626→      // Event log (only when dirty)
   627→      renderEventLog();
   628→    }
   629→
   630→    // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   631→
   632→    initObjectCards();
   633→    initCharacterCards();
   634→    requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   635→  </script>
   636→</body>
   637→</html>
   638→

  "new_string": "class ObjectInstance {\n  constructor(def) {\n    this.id        = def.id;\n    this.name      = def.name;\n    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine\n    this.position  = def.position;\n    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks\n    this.ty        = def.position.ty;\n    this.states    = def.states;\n    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';\n    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;\n    this.autoTimer = 0;\n    this._resetAutoTimer();\n\n    // Slot system\n    this.capacity      = def.capacity ?? 1;\n    this._reservations = new Set(); // charNames walking toward this object\n    this._occupants    = new Set(); // charNames actively interacting\n  }\n\n  /** True if no more slots are available (reserved + occupied >= capacity). */\n  isFull() {\n    return this._reservations.size + this._occupants.size >= this.capacity;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Reserve a slot for charName before they start walking.\n   * Returns true if the reservation succeeded, false if the object is full.\n   */\n  reserve(charName) {\n    if (this.isFull()) return false;\n    this._reservations.add(charName);\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Called when charName arrives at the object.\n   * Converts the reservation to an active occupancy.\n   */\n  arrive(charName) {\n    this._reservations.delete(charName);\n    this._occupants.add(charName);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Release a slot when the character finishes interacting or abandons the walk.\n   */\n  release(charName) {\n    this._reservations.delete(charName);\n    this._occupants.delete(charName);\n  }\n\n  /** Clear all reservations and occupancies (used on sim reset). */\n  clearSlots() {\n    this._reservations.clear();\n    this._occupants.clear();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Returns current slot occupancy info.\n   * @returns {{ capacity, reserved, occupied, available }}\n   */\n  getSlotInfo() {\n    return {\n      capacity:  this.capacity,\n      reserved:  this._reservations.size,\n      occupied:  this._occupants.size,\n      available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size,\n    };\n  }"

   215→
   216→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   217→
   218→class ObjectInstance {
   219→  constructor(def) {
   220→    this.id        = def.id;
   221→    this.name      = def.name;
   222→    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   223→    this.position  = def.position;
   224→    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   225→    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   226→    this.states    = def.states;
   227→    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   228→    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   229→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   230→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   231→
   232→    // Slot system
   233→    this.capacity      = def.capacity ?? 1;
   234→    this._reservations = new Set(); // charNames walking toward this object
   235→    this._occupants    = new Set(); // charNames actively interacting
   236→  }
   237→
   238→  /** True if no more slots are available (reserved + occupied >= capacity). */
   239→  isFull() {
   240→    return this._reservations.size + this._occupants.size >= this.capacity;
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  /**
   244→   * Reserve a slot for charName before they start walking.
   245→   * Returns true if the reservation succeeded, false if the object is full.
   246→   */
   247→  reserve(charName) {
   248→    if (this.isFull()) return false;
   249→    this._reservations.add(charName);
   250→    return true;
   251→  }
   252→
   253→  /**
   254→   * Called when charName arrives at the object.
   255→   * Converts the reservation to an active occupancy.
   256→   */
   257→  arrive(charName) {
   258→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   259→    this._occupants.add(charName);
   260→  }
   261→
   262→  /**
   263→   * Release a slot when the character finishes interacting or abandons the walk.
   264→   */
   265→  release(charName) {
   266→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   267→    this._occupants.delete(charName);
   268→  }
   269→
   270→  /** Clear all reservations and occupancies (used on sim reset). */
   271→  clearSlots() {
   272→    this._reservations.clear();
   273→    this._occupants.clear();
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  /**
   277→   * Returns current slot occupancy info.
   278→   * @returns {{ capacity, reserved, occupied, available }}
   279→   */
   280→  getSlotInfo() {
   281→    return {
   282→      capacity:  this.capacity,
   283→      reserved:  this._reservations.size,
   284→      occupied:  this._occupants.size,
   285→      available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size,
   286→    };
   287→  }
   288→
   289→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   290→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   291→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   292→  }
   293→
   294→  /**
   295→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   296→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   297→   */
   298→  interact(action = 'use') {
   299→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   300→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   301→    if (!tr) return null;
   302→
   303→    this.state = tr.next;
   304→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   305→
   306→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   307→    return {
   308→      objectId: this.id,
   309→      state:    this.state,
   310→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   311→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   312→    };
   313→  }
   314→
   315→  /**
   316→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   317→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   318→   */
   319→  tick(deltaMs) {
   320→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   321→
   322→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   323→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   324→
   325→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   326→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   327→
   328→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   329→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   330→
   331→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   332→    return {
   333→      objectId: this.id,
   334→      state:    this.state,
   335→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   336→      auto:     true,
   337→    };
   338→  }
   339→}
   340→
   341→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   342→
   343→export class ObjectEngine {
   344→  constructor() {
   345→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   346→  }
   347→
   348→  addObjects(defs) {
   349→    for (const def of defs) {
   350→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   351→    }
   352→  }
   353→
   354→  /**
   355→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   356→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   357→   */
   358→  tick(deltaMs) {
   359→    const events = [];
   360→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   361→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   362→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   363→    }
   364→    return events;
   365→  }
   366→
   367→  /**
   368→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   369→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   370→   */
   371→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   372→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   373→  }
   374→
   375→  getAll()    { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   376→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   377→
   378→  reserve(objectId, charName) { return this._map.get(objectId)?.reserve(charName) ?? false; }
   379→  arrive(objectId, charName)  { this._map.get(objectId)?.arrive(charName); }
   380→  release(objectId, charName) { this._map.get(objectId)?.release(charName); }
   381→  clearSlots(objectId)        { this._map.get(objectId)?.clearSlots(); }
   382→  clearAllSlots()             { for (const obj of this._map.values()) obj.clearSlots(); }
   383→}

     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).

     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();

    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)

    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions
    67→      const prevAction        = char.action;
    68→      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;
    69→
    70→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    72→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    76→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    77→        this._doWander(char);
    78→      }
    79→
    80→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    81→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    82→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    83→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    84→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    85→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    86→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    87→        }
    88→      }
    89→
    90→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    91→      char.update(deltaMs);
    92→

    94→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
    95→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
    96→      }
    97→    }
    98→  }
    99→
   100→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   101→
   102→  /**
   103→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   104→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   105→   */
   106→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   107→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   108→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
   109→
   110→    if (event) {
   111→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   112→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   113→
   114→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   115→
   116→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   117→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   118→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   119→      if (obj && event.state) {
   120→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   121→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   122→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   123→        }
   124→      }
   125→
   126→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs);
   127→
   128→      if (event.speech) {
   129→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   130→      }
   131→
   132→      if (event.emoji) {
   133→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   134→      }
   135→    } else {
   136→      // No valid transition — release the reservation
   137→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   138→    }
   139→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   140→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   141→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   142→  }
   143→
   144→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   145→
   146→  _doWander(char) {
   147→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   148→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   149→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   150→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   151→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   152→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   153→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   154→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   155→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   156→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   157→            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking
   158→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   159→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   160→            return;
   161→          }
   162→        }
   163→        // All objects full or unreachable — fall through to random wander
   164→      }
   165→    }
   166→
   167→    // Random walkable tile
   168→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   169→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   170→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   171→      return;
   172→    }
   173→
   174→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   175→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   176→
   177→    let moved = false;
   178→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   179→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   180→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   181→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   182→      if (moved) break;
   183→    }
   184→
   185→    if (!moved) {
   186→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   187→    }
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  /**
   191→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   192→   */
   193→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   194→    const dirs = [
   195→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   196→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   197→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   198→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   199→    ];
   200→    for (const d of dirs) {
   201→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   202→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   203→      }
   204→    }
   205→    return null;
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   209→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   210→    const tiles = [];
   211→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   212→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   213→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   214→      }
   215→    }
   216→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   217→    return tiles;
   218→  }
   219→
   220→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   221→
   222→  getSimTimeString() {
   223→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   224→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   225→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   226→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   227→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   228→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   229→  }
   230→}
   231→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #109
The code looks good. Now let me think about one potential issue I see: In `_doWander`, the order is: 1. `if (obj.isFull()) continue;` 2. `const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);` 3. `if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {` 4. `obj.reserve(char.name);` The `moveTo` call happens BEFORE `reserve`. But `moveTo` just sets the path on the character — it doesn't actually interact with the object engine. The reservation needs to happen atomically with the commitment to walk. Since JavaScript is single-threaded, the frame processes all characters sequentially. So if Char A runs _doWander first and calls `obj.reserve('Maple')`, then Char B runs _doWander and calls `obj.isFull()` → true → skips. Actually, the `moveTo` call is already guarded by the check that it succeeds before we reserve, so if movement fails we don't reserve. And since each character's entire `_doWander` completes before the next one starts in a single-threaded environment, two characters can't both see the object as not full and then both reserve it — whichever runs first will reserve and fill it, blocking the second. I'll leave the hardcoded "Objects (10)" title as is and check if there's anything else in scene.js that needs attention.

    47→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    48→  const grid = [];
    49→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    50→    const r = [];
    51→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    52→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    53→    }
    54→    grid.push(r);
    55→  }
    56→  // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
    57→  for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
    58→    const { tx, ty } = def.position;
    59→    if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}

   451→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   452→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   453→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   454→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   455→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   456→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   457→      if (!badge) return;
   458→
   459→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   460→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   461→
   462→      if (stateChanged) {
   463→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   464→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   465→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   466→
   467→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   468→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   469→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   470→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   471→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   472→        ).join('');
   473→      }
   474→
   475→      // Slot occupancy (update every frame)
   476→      const slotDiv = document.getElementById(`slots-${obj.id}`);
   477→      if (slotDiv) {
   478→        const si = obj.getSlotInfo();
   479→        const pips = [];
   480→        for (let i = 0; i < si.capacity; i++) {
   481→          let cls = 'available';
   482→          if (i < si.occupied)                      cls = 'occupied';
   483→          else if (i < si.occupied + si.reserved)   cls = 'reserved';
   484→          pips.push(`<div class="slot-pip ${cls}" title="${cls}"></div>`);
   485→        }
   486→        const labelCls = si.available === 0 ? 'slot-label full' : 'slot-label';
   487→        const labelTxt = si.available === 0 ? 'full' : `${si.available}/${si.capacity} free`;
   488→        slotDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="slot-pips">${pips.join('')}</div><span class="${labelCls}">${labelTxt}</span>`;
   489→      }
   490→
   491→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   492→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   493→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   494→      if (hasTimer) {
   495→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   496→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   497→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   498→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   499→        timerText.style.display = '';

}\n  reserve(name)    { if (this.isFull()) return false; this._reservations.add(name); return true; }\n  arrive(name)     { this._reservations.delete(name); this._occupants.add(name); }\n  release(name)    { this._reservations.delete(name); this._occupants.delete(name); }\n  clearSlots()     { this._reservations.clear(); this._occupants.clear(); }\n  getSlotInfo()    { return { capacity: this.capacity, reserved: this._reservations.size, occupied: this._occupants.size, available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size }; }\n}\n\n// Test capacity-1 object\nconst teaSet = new ObjectInstance(1);\nconsole.assert(teaSet.reserve('Maple') === true, 'Maple can reserve empty object');\nconsole.assert(teaSet.reserve('Sol')   === false, 'Sol cannot reserve full object');\nconsole.assert(teaSet.isFull()         === true,  'Object is full after 1 reservation');\nteaSet.arrive('Maple');\nconsole.assert(teaSet._reservations.size === 0, 'Reservation cleared on arrive');\nconsole.assert(teaSet._occupants.size   === 1, 'Occupant added on arrive');\nteaSet.release('Maple');\nconsole.assert(teaSet.isFull()           === false, 'Object free after release');\nconsole.assert(teaSet.reserve('Sol')     === true,  'Sol can reserve after release');\n\n// Test capacity-2 object\nconst kotatsu = new ObjectInstance(2);\nconsole.assert(kotatsu.reserve('Maple') === true, 'First reservation OK');\nconsole.assert(kotatsu.reserve('Sol')   === true, 'Second reservation OK');\nconsole.assert(kotatsu.reserve('Nyx')   === false,'Third reservation blocked');\nkotatsu.arrive('Maple'); kotatsu.arrive('Sol');\nkotatsu.release('Maple');\nconsole.assert(kotatsu.reserve('Nyx')   === true, 'Slot opens after release');\n\n// Test getSlotInfo\nconst info = kotatsu.getSlotInfo();\nconsole.assert(info.capacity === 2, 'Capacity correct');\nconsole.assert(info.occupied === 1, 'Occupied count correct');\nconsole.assert(info.reserved === 1, 'Reserved count correct');\nconsole.assert(info.available === 0, 'Available count correct');\n\nconsole.log('All slot system tests passed!');\n\"\n"

  "command": "gh pr create \\\n  --title \"feat: interaction slot system \u2014 smart objects enforce capacity (FRG-222)\" \\\n  --body \"$(cat <<'EOF'\n## Summary\n\n- Objects now have configurable `capacity` (max simultaneous users): kotatsu & TV = 2, all others = 1\n- Characters check slot availability before walking to an object; full objects are skipped\n- Reservation \u2192 occupancy lifecycle: `reserve()` when committing to walk, `arrive()` on arrival, `release()` when interaction timer expires\n- AIEngine includes slot availability in the LLM prompt so the AI makes capacity-aware decisions\n- Debug page shows per-object slot occupancy as coloured pips (orange = active, grey = reserved, dark = free)\n\n## How it works\n\n**Reservation lifecycle:**\n1. Character decides to visit an object \u2192 `obj.reserve(charName)` \u2192 returns false if full (skip to another object)\n2. Character arrives at adjacent tile \u2192 `obj.arrive(charName)` converts reservation to occupancy\n3. Interaction timer expires \u2192 `obj.release(charName)` frees the slot\n\n**Concurrency safe:** JS is single-threaded so the synchronous `reserve()` call is atomic within a frame \u2014 two characters processed in the same frame cannot double-book the same slot.\n\n**Stale reservation cleanup:** If AIEngine reassigns a character to a different object while walking, the old reservation is released before the new one is created.\n\n## Test plan\n- [ ] Open `debug.html` and observe slot pips on object cards\n- [ ] Verify capacity-1 objects (tea_set, stove, etc.) never show two characters interacting simultaneously\n- [ ] Verify capacity-2 objects (kotatsu, TV) allow up to two characters\n- [ ] Verify \"full\" label appears in red when all slots are taken\n- [ ] Click Reset \u2014 slot pips return to all-empty\n- [ ] AI mode: confirm LLM prompt includes `slots` field; characters avoid full objects\n\nCloses FRG-222\n\n\ud83e\udd16 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\nEOF\n)\" \\\n  --base master 2>&1"

{"id":"e92573fd-6811-4820-9777-8ab495a143e5","identifier":"FRG-222","title":"Interaction Slot System (Smart Objects)","description":"Objects must be service providers with capacity and reservation logic.

## Current Problem

Multiple characters can walk to and interact with the same object simultaneously. No conflict detection — tea_set can be 'used' by all 3 characters at once.

## Requirements

1. **Slots/Capacity:** Each object defines how many characters can use it simultaneously (e.g., bench=2, single chair=1, tea_set=1, kotatsu=2).
2. **Reservation:** Before walking to an object, character must request a reservation. Object returns available/busy.
3. **State Locking:** Once character arrives and begins interaction, slot is locked. Other characters checking that object get a 'busy' signal.
4. **Release:** When interaction ends (auto_next timer expires), slot is released.

## Acceptance Criteria

* Objects have configurable capacity (slots)
* Characters check availability before committing to an interaction
* If object is full, character receives busy signal and must choose differently
* Debug page shows slot occupancy per object
* No two characters interact with a capacity-1 object simultaneously","projectMilestone":{"id":"d98e487a-66f2-4106-86d3-550aac4cb898","name":"M1: Sim engine correct (debug foundation)"},"priority":{"value":1,"name":"Urgent"},"url":"https://linear.app/chills-linear/issue/FRG-222/interaction-slot-system-smart-objects","gitBranchName":"chillkimtest/frg-222-interaction-slot-system-smart-objects","createdAt":"2026-03-07T17:41:11.312Z","updatedAt":"2026-03-07T17:59:47.890Z","archivedAt":null,"completedAt":null,"dueDate":null,"slaStartedAt":null,"slaMediumRiskAt":null,"slaHighRiskAt":null,"slaBreachesAt":null,"slaType":"all","status":"Test in Progress","labels":[],"attachments":[{"id":"805eca7a-9e2f-48d3-bb7d-c2e772d74fdf","title":"feat: interaction slot system — smart objects enforce capacity (FRG-222)","subtitle":null,"url":"https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/8"}],"documents":[],"createdBy":"Chill","createdById":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","assignee":"Chill","assigneeId":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","project":"AI Aquarium","projectId":"0385a8c7-ba5a-43a3-b223-acf4d1ad6d63","team":"Forge","teamId":"c3ef97d8-21a8-4aa7-a818-298f217864dd"}

Other characters checking that object get a 'busy' signal.\\n4. **Release:** When interaction ends (auto_next timer expires), slot is released.\\n\\n## Acceptance Criteria\\n\\n* Objects have configurable capacity (slots)\\n* Characters check availability before committing to an interaction\\n* If object is full, character receives busy signal and must choose differently\\n* Debug page shows slot occupancy per object\\n* No two characters interact with a capacity-1 object simultaneously\",\"projectMilestone\":{\"id\":\"d98e487a-66f2-4106-86d3-550aac4cb898\",\"name\":\"M1: Sim engine correct (debug foundation)\"},\"priority\":{\"value\":1,\"name\":\"Urgent\"},\"url\":\"https://linear.app/chills-linear/issue/FRG-222/interaction-slot-system-smart-objects\",\"gitBranchName\":\"chillkimtest/frg-222-interaction-slot-system-smart-objects\",\"createdAt\":\"2026-03-07T17:41:11.312Z\",\"updatedAt\":\"2026-03-07T17:59:47.890Z\",\"archivedAt\":null,\"completedAt\":null,\"dueDate\":null,\"slaStartedAt\":null,\"slaMediumRiskAt\":null,\"slaHighRiskAt\":null,\"slaBreachesAt\":null,\"slaType\":\"all\",\"status\":\"Test in Progress\",\"labels\":[],\"attachments\":[{\"id\":\"805eca7a-9e2f-48d3-bb7d-c2e772d74fdf\",\"title\":\"feat: interaction slot system \u2014 smart objects enforce capacity (FRG-222)\",\"subtitle\":null,\"url\":\"https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/8\"}],\"documents\":[],\"createdBy\":\"Chill\",\"createdById\":\"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7\",\"assignee\":\"Chill\",\"assigneeId\":\"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7\",\"project\":\"AI Aquarium\",\"projectId\":\"0385a8c7-ba5a-43a3-b223-acf4d1ad6d63\",\"team\":\"Forge\",\"teamId\":\"c3ef97d8-21a8-4aa7-a818-298f217864dd\"}"

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #139
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/objects.js` — Added `capacity` field to all 10 `OBJECT_DEFS` (kotatsu & TV = 2, rest = 1); added `isFull()`, `reserve()`, `arrive()`, `release()`, `clearSlots()`, `getSlotInfo()` to `ObjectInstance`; added passthrough methods on `ObjectEngine` - `src/Engine.js` — `_doWander` now skips full objects and calls `reserve()` before committing; `_handleObjectArrival` calls `arrive()` on success and `release()` on no-transition; update loop detects interacting→idle transition and releases the slot - `src/AIEngine.js` — Nearby objects in the LLM prompt now include `slots` availability info; `_applyDecision` checks `isFull()` before reserving and cleans up stale reservations when reassigning targets - `debug.html` — Object cards now show pip-based slot occupancy (orange = occupied, grey = reserved, dark = free); reset button clears all slot state; added CSS for slot pips ## Key Decisions - **Reserve-then-arrive pattern**: Characters hold a reservation while walking (blocking others) which converts to an occupancy on arrival — this prevents the race where two characters both commit to the same full object in the same frame - **JS single-threaded safety**: `reserve()` modifies the Set immediately, so sequential character processing within one frame naturally prevents double-booking without locks - **Stale reservation cleanup in AIEngine**: When the AI re-routes a walking character to a different object, the old reservation is explicitly released to avoid slot leaks ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/FRG-222-interaction-slot-system` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/8
